***затея.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затея.html>зате́я</a> (6346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Attested first from the year 1771, of unknown provenance; it is not known whether <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">-за-</span> is a prefix and what the <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">-тѣй-</span> part could be.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затея.html>зате́я</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatéja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затея.html>зате́и</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затея.html>зате́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затеять.html>зате́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>enterprise, undertaking</li>
<li><i>(usually plural)</i> piece of fun, fancy</li></ol>

***затеять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затеять.html>зате́ять</a> (5945)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">заце́яць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zacjéjacʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to undertake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and (with a different prefix) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">ви́тіяти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výtijaty</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to undertake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Per Vasmer, the base verb (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tějati</i>) is possibly related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">tievêt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to strive for</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">tĩtît</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be stubborn, to be annoyed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1sg. <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">tĩtĩju</i>), <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">tītinât</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tease, to annoy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">titinoti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to brag</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затеять.html>зате́ять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatéjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затевать.html>затева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to undertake, to start
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затеять.html>зате́ять</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:недобрый.html>недо́брое</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatéjatʹ</b> nedóbroje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to misbehave, to be up to no good</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затеять.html>зате́ять</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:драка.html>дра́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatéjatʹ</b> dráku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to start a fight</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to decide (to do something)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to venture</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>те́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ять</b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затихнуть.html>зати́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatíxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затихать.html>затиха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatixátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затихнуть.html>зати́хнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become silent, to become quiet, to stop speaking, to stop crying</li>
<li>to die away, to die off</li>
<li>to calm down, to abate, to subside, to lull</li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затихнуть.html>зати́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatíxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затихать.html>затиха́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become silent, to become quiet, to stop speaking, to stop crying</li>
<li>to die away, to die off</li>
<li>to calm down, to abate, to subside, to lull</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***заткнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заткнуть.html>заткну́ть</a> (7322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ткнуть.html>ткнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заткнуть.html>заткну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatknútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затыкать.html>затыка́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stop up, to plug, to cork
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заткнуть.html>заткну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дыра.html>дыры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatknútʹ</b> dyry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fill in holes, close gaps</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заткнуть.html>заткну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рота.html>рот</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatknútʹ</b> rot</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to silence, stop someone's mouth, stop blabbing, shut up</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to stick, to thrust
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заткнуть.html>заткну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пояс.html>по́яс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatknútʹ</b> za pójas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be one too many, to go one better than</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***заткнуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заткнуться.html>заткну́ться</a> (7552)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заткнуть.html>заткну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заткнуться.html>заткну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatknútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">затыка́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be stopped, to be corked</li>
<li>to shut up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">stop talking</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заткнуть.html>заткну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Please note that saying “shut up” is regarded as much more rude in Russia. Take caution.</li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***затмевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затмевать.html>затмева́ть</a> (30890)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затмить.html>затми́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatmítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ева́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затмевать.html>затмева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatmevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затмить.html>затми́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to obscure, to make invisible, to eclipse
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b>затмева́т</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatmevát</b> glazá jemú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is being deprived of the opportunity to see</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to obscure, to make unclear <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. thoughts</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to outshine</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to eclipse, to surpass, to outdo, to outshine</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затмить.html>затми́ть</a> (20901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">тмить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tmitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затмить.html>затми́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatmítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затмевать.html>затмева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to obscure, to make invisible, to eclipse
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затмить.html>затми́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatmílo</b> glazá jemú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was deprived of the opportunity to see</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to obscure, to make unclear <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. thoughts</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to outshine</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to eclipse, to surpass, to outdo, to outshine</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затоптать.html>затопта́ть</a> (12224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топтать.html>топта́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">toptátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затоптать.html>затопта́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatoptátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зата́птывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to trample down, to trample under foot</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тормозить.html>тормози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tormozítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
